<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Label</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Area</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Input</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Preview</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Area</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Control</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.EditTrigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.SubmitTrigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> props to control the editable state.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the editable is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useEditable</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the editable&#x27;s state with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Editable.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useEditableContext</code> hook—great for showing keyboard hints
when editing.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controls" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controls"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controls</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In some cases, you might need to use custom controls to toggle the edit and read mode. We use the render prop pattern to
provide access to the internal state of the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="textarea" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#textarea"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Textarea</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">asChild</code> prop on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Editable.Input</code> to render a textarea for multi-line editing.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of an editable. It includes handling
ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="auto-resizing" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#auto-resizing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Auto-resizing</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To auto-grow the editable as the content changes, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autoResize</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> placeholder</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;Placeholder&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> autoResize</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  {</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/*...*/</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="max-length" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#max-length"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Max Length</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxLength</code> prop to set a maximum number of characters that can be entered into the editable.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> placeholder</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;Placeholder&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> autoResize</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> maxLength</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">10</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  {</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/*...*/</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="double-click" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#double-click"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Double Click</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The editable supports two modes of activating the &quot;edit&quot; state:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">when the preview part is focused (with pointer or keyboard).</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">when the preview part is double-clicked.</li>
</ul>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To change the mode to double-click, pass the prop <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">activationMode=&quot;dblclick&quot;</code>.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> placeholder</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;Placeholder&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> activationMode</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;dblclick&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  {</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/*...*/</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Editable.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;div&gt;</code> element.</p><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Prop</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Default</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">activationMode</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&#x27;focus&#x27;</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">ActivationMode</code><p class="text">The activation mode for the preview element.

- &quot;focus&quot; - Enter edit mode when the preview is focused
- &quot;dblclick&quot; - Enter edit mode when the preview is double-clicked
- &quot;click&quot; - Enter edit mode when the preview is clicked
- &quot;none&quot; - Edit can be triggered programmatically only</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell <h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>
<div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Enter</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Saves the edited content and exits edit mode.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"editable\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cEditable.Root\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Label /\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Input /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Preview /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Control\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.EditTrigger /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.SubmitTrigger /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.CancelTrigger /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/react/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root className={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area className={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview className={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.EditTrigger className={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/solid/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/vue/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area :class=\"styles.Area\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview :class=\"styles.Preview\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.EditTrigger :class=\"styles.EditTrigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Editable } from '@ark-ui/svelte/editable'\n  import PencilIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/pencil'\n  import styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n      \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nUse the `value` and `onValueChange` props to control the editable state.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/react/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = useState('Hello World')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cEditable.Root\n      className={styles.Root}\n      placeholder=\"Enter text...\"\n      value={value}\n      onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setValue(e.value)}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Area className={styles.Area}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Preview className={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.EditTrigger className={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/solid/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = createSignal('Hello World')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cEditable.Root\n      class={styles.Root}\n      placeholder=\"Enter text...\"\n      value={value()}\n      onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setValue(e.value)}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/vue/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nconst value = ref('Hello World')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" placeholder=\"Enter text...\" v-model=\"value\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area :class=\"styles.Area\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview :class=\"styles.Preview\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.EditTrigger :class=\"styles.EditTrigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Editable } from '@ark-ui/svelte/editable'\n  import PencilIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/pencil'\n  import styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\n  let value = $state('Hello World')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter text...\" {value} onValueChange={(e) =\u003e (value = e.value)}\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n      \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the editable is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useEditable` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable, useEditable } from '@ark-ui/react/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const editable = useEditable({ defaultValue: 'Hello World' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cEditable.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={editable}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Area className={styles.Area}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Preview className={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.EditTrigger className={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable, useEditable } from '@ark-ui/solid/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const editable = useEditable({ defaultValue: 'Hello World' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cEditable.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={editable}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Editable, useEditable } from '@ark-ui/vue/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nconst editable = useEditable({ defaultValue: 'Hello World' })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"editable\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area :class=\"styles.Area\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview :class=\"styles.Preview\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.EditTrigger :class=\"styles.EditTrigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Editable, useEditable } from '@ark-ui/svelte/editable'\n  import PencilIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/pencil'\n  import styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\n  const editable = useEditable({ defaultValue: 'Hello World' })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cEditable.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={editable}\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n      \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Editable.RootProvider\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nAccess the editable's state with `Editable.Context` or the `useEditableContext` hook—great for showing keyboard hints\nwhen editing.\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/react/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root className={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area className={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview className={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Context\u003e\n      {(editable) =\u003e\n        editable.editing ? (\n          \u003cspan className={styles.HelperText}\u003eEnter to save, Esc to cancel\u003c/span\u003e\n        ) : (\n          \u003cEditable.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n            \u003cEditable.EditTrigger className={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n          \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n        )\n      }\n    \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/solid/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Show } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Context\u003e\n      {(editable) =\u003e (\n        \u003cShow\n          when={editable().editing}\n          fallback={\n            \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n              \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n          }\n        \u003e\n          \u003cspan class={styles.HelperText}\u003eEnter to save, Esc to cancel\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/Show\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/vue/editable'\nimport { PencilIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area :class=\"styles.Area\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview :class=\"styles.Preview\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Context v-slot=\"{ editing }\"\u003e\n      \u003cspan v-if=\"editing\" :class=\"styles.HelperText\"\u003eEnter to save, Esc to cancel\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Control v-else :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.EditTrigger :class=\"styles.EditTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Editable } from '@ark-ui/svelte/editable'\n  import PencilIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/pencil'\n  import styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter text...\" defaultValue=\"Hello World\"\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(editable)}\n      {#if editable().editing}\n        \u003cspan class={styles.HelperText}\u003eEnter to save, Esc to cancel\u003c/span\u003e\n      {:else}\n        \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n      {/if}\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controls\n\nIn some cases, you might need to use custom controls to toggle the edit and read mode. We use the render prop pattern to\nprovide access to the internal state of the component.\n\n**Example: controls**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/react/editable'\nimport { CheckIcon, PencilIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Controls = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"Click edit to start\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area className={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview className={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Context\u003e\n      {(editable) =\u003e (\n        \u003cEditable.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          {editable.editing ? (\n            \u003c\u003e\n              \u003cEditable.SubmitTrigger className={styles.SubmitTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Editable.SubmitTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cEditable.CancelTrigger className={styles.CancelTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Editable.CancelTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/\u003e\n          ) : (\n            \u003cEditable.EditTrigger className={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/solid/editable'\nimport { CheckIcon, PencilIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Show } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Controls = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"Click edit to start\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Context\u003e\n      {(editable) =\u003e (\n        \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cShow\n            when={editable().editing}\n            fallback={\n              \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n            }\n          \u003e\n            \u003cEditable.SubmitTrigger class={styles.SubmitTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Editable.SubmitTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cEditable.CancelTrigger class={styles.CancelTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Editable.CancelTrigger\u003e\n          \u003c/Show\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/vue/editable'\nimport { CheckIcon, PencilIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" defaultValue=\"Click edit to start\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area :class=\"styles.Area\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview :class=\"styles.Preview\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Context v-slot=\"{ editing }\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003ctemplate v-if=\"editing\"\u003e\n          \u003cEditable.SubmitTrigger :class=\"styles.SubmitTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Editable.SubmitTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cEditable.CancelTrigger :class=\"styles.CancelTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Editable.CancelTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.EditTrigger v-else :class=\"styles.EditTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Editable } from '@ark-ui/svelte/editable'\n  import CheckIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/check'\n  import PencilIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/pencil'\n  import XIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/x'\n  import styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"Click edit to start\"\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(editable)}\n      \u003cEditable.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        {#if editable().editing}\n          \u003cEditable.SubmitTrigger class={styles.SubmitTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Editable.SubmitTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cEditable.CancelTrigger class={styles.CancelTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Editable.CancelTrigger\u003e\n        {:else}\n          \u003cEditable.EditTrigger class={styles.EditTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cPencilIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Editable.EditTrigger\u003e\n        {/if}\n      \u003c/Editable.Control\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Editable.Context\u003e\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Textarea\n\nUse the `asChild` prop on `Editable.Input` to render a textarea for multi-line editing.\n\n**Example: textarea**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/react/editable'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Textarea = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root\n    className={styles.Root}\n    placeholder=\"Enter a description...\"\n    defaultValue=\"Ark UI is a headless component library for building reusable, scalable design systems.\"\n    activationMode=\"dblclick\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eDescription\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area className={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input className={styles.Textarea} asChild\u003e\n        \u003ctextarea /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Input\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview className={styles.Textarea} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.HelperText}\u003ePress Cmd + Enter to save\u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/solid/editable'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const Textarea = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cEditable.Root\n    class={styles.Root}\n    placeholder=\"Enter a description...\"\n    defaultValue=\"Ark UI is a headless component library for building reusable, scalable design systems.\"\n    activationMode=\"dblclick\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eDescription\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Textarea} asChild={(props) =\u003e \u003ctextarea {...props()} /\u003e} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Textarea} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.HelperText}\u003ePress Cmd + Enter to save\u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/vue/editable'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Root\n    :class=\"styles.Root\"\n    placeholder=\"Enter a description...\"\n    defaultValue=\"Ark UI is a headless component library for building reusable, scalable design systems.\"\n    activationMode=\"dblclick\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eDescription\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area :class=\"styles.Area\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input :class=\"styles.Textarea\" asChild\u003e\n        \u003ctextarea /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Input\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview :class=\"styles.Textarea\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.HelperText\"\u003ePress Cmd + Enter to save\u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Editable } from '@ark-ui/svelte/editable'\n  import styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cEditable.Root\n  class={styles.Root}\n  placeholder=\"Enter a description...\"\n  defaultValue=\"Ark UI is a headless component library for building reusable, scalable design systems.\"\n  activationMode=\"dblclick\"\n\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eDescription\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Textarea}\u003e\n      {#snippet asChild(props)}\n        \u003ctextarea {...props()}\u003e\u003c/textarea\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Editable.Input\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Textarea} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.HelperText}\u003ePress Cmd + Enter to save\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nThe `Field` component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of an editable. It includes handling\nARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/react/editable'\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Root className={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter your bio\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Label className={field.Label}\u003eBio\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Area className={styles.Area}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Preview className={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText className={field.HelperText}\u003eClick to edit your bio\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText className={field.ErrorText}\u003eBio is required\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/solid/editable'\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter your bio\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Label class={field.Label}\u003eBio\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eDouble-click to edit your bio\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eBio is required\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Editable } from '@ark-ui/vue/editable'\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cField.Root :class=\"field.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" placeholder=\"Enter your bio\"\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Label :class=\"field.Label\"\u003eBio\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Area :class=\"styles.Area\"\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n        \u003cEditable.Preview :class=\"styles.Preview\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText :class=\"field.HelperText\"\u003eDouble-click to edit your bio\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText :class=\"field.ErrorText\"\u003eBio is required\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Editable } from '@ark-ui/svelte/editable'\n  import { Field } from '@ark-ui/svelte/field'\n  import field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/editable.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cEditable.Root class={styles.Root} placeholder=\"Enter your bio\"\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Label class={field.Label}\u003eBio\u003c/Editable.Label\u003e\n    \u003cEditable.Area class={styles.Area}\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cEditable.Preview class={styles.Preview} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Editable.Area\u003e\n  \u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n  \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eDouble-click to edit your bio\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n  \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eBio is required\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n\u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n## Guides\n\n### Auto-resizing\n\nTo auto-grow the editable as the content changes, set the `autoResize` prop to `true`.\n\n```tsx\n\u003cEditable.Root placeholder=\"Placeholder\" autoResize\u003e\n  {/*...*/}\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n```\n\n### Max Length\n\nUse the `maxLength` prop to set a maximum number of characters that can be entered into the editable.\n\n```tsx\n\u003cEditable.Root placeholder=\"Placeholder\" autoResize maxLength={10}\u003e\n  {/*...*/}\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n```\n\n### Double Click\n\nThe editable supports two modes of activating the \"edit\" state:\n\n- when the preview part is focused (with pointer or keyboard).\n- when the preview part is double-clicked.\n\nTo change the mode to double-click, pass the prop `activationMode=\"dblclick\"`.\n\n```tsx\n\u003cEditable.Root placeholder=\"Placeholder\" activationMode=\"dblclick\"\u003e\n  {/*...*/}\n\u003c/Editable.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `activationMode` | `ActivationMode` | No | The activation mode for the preview element.\n\n- \"focus\" - Enter edit mode when the preview is focused\n- \"dblclick\" - Enter edit mode when the preview is double-clicked\n- \"click\" - Enter edit mode when the preview is clicked\n- \"none\" - Edit can be triggered programmatically only |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `autoResize` | `boolean` | No | Whether the editable should auto-resize to fit the content. |\n| `defaultEdit` | `boolean` | No | Whether the editable is in edit mode by default. |\n| `defaultValue` | `string` | No | The initial value of the editable when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the editable. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the editable is disabled. |\n| `edit` | `boolean` | No | Whether the editable is in edit mode. |\n| `finalFocusEl` | `() =\u003e HTMLElement | null` | No | The element to receive focus when the editable is closed. |\n| `form` | `string` | No | The associate form of the underlying input. |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  area: string\n  label: string\n  preview: string\n  input: string\n  control: string\n  submitTrigger: string\n  cancelTrigger: string\n  editTrigger: string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the editable. Useful for composition. |\n| `invalid` | `boolean` | No | Whether the input's value is invalid. |\n| `maxLength` | `number` | No | The maximum number of characters allowed in the editable |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name attribute of the editable component.
